Calling\n194: // InstallPathHandler more than once for the same path and mux will\n195: // result in a panic.\n196: func InstallPathHandler(mux mux, path string, checks ...HealthChecker) {\n197: \tInstallPathHandlerWithHealthyFunc(mux, path, nil, checks...)\n198: }\n199: \n200: // InstallPathHandlerWithHealthyFunc is like InstallPathHandler, but calls firstTimeHealthy exactly once\n201: // when the handler succeeds for the first time.\n202: func InstallPathHandlerWithHealthyFunc(mux mux, path string, firstTimeHealthy func(), checks ...HealthChecker) {\n203: \tif len(checks) == 0 {\n204: \t\tklog.V(5).Info(\"No default health checks specified. Installing the ping handler.\")\n205: \t\tchecks = []HealthChecker{PingHealthz}\n206: \t}\n207: \n208: \tklog.V(5).Infof(\"Installing health checkers for (%v): %v\", path, \tfor _, check := range checks {\n223: \t\tmux.Handle(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s/%v\", path, check.Name()), adaptCheckToHandler(check.Check))\n224: \t}\n225: }\n226: \n227: // mux is an interface describing the methods InstallHandler requires.\n228: type mux interface {\n229: \tHandle(pattern string, handler http.Handler)\n230: }\n231: \n232: // healthzCheck implements HealthChecker on an arbitrary name and check function.\n233: type healthzCheck struct {\n234: \tname  string\n235: \tcheck func(r *http.Request) error\n236: }\n237: \n238: var _ HealthChecker = &healthzCheck{}\n239: \n240: func (c \treturn c.groupName\n257: }\n258: \n259: // getExcludedChecks extracts the health check names to be excluded from the query param\n260: func getExcludedChecks(r *http.Request) sets.String {\n261: \tchecks, found := r.URL.Query()[\"exclude\"]\n262: \tif found {\n263: \t\treturn sets.NewString(checks...)\n264: \t}\n265: \treturn sets.NewString()\n266: }\n267: \n268: // handleRootHealth returns an http.HandlerFunc that serves the provided checks.\n269: func handleRootHealth(name string, firstTimeHealthy func(), checks ...HealthChecker) http.HandlerFunc {\n270: \tvar notifyOnce sync.Once\n271: \treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n272: \t\texcluded := getExcludedChecks(r)\n273: \t\tunknownExcluded := excluded.Clone()\n274: \t\t// failedVerboseLogOutput is for output to the log.  It indicates detailed failed output information for the log.\n275: \t\tvar failedVerboseLogOutput bytes.Buffer\n276: \t\tvar failedChecks []string\n277: \t\tvar individualCheckOutput bytes.Buffer\n278: \t\tfor _, check := range checks {\n279: \t\t\t// no-op the check if we've specified we want to exclude the check\n280: \t\t\tif excluded.Has(check.Name()) {\n281: \t\t\t\tunknownExcluded.Delete(check.Name())\n282: \t\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(&individualCheckOutput, \"[+]%s excluded: ok\\n\", check.Name())\n283: \t\t\t\tcontinue\n284: \t\t\t}\n285: \t\t\t// no-op the check if it is a grouped check and we want to exclude the group\n286: \t\t\tif check, ok := check.(GroupedHealthChecker); ok && excluded.Has(check.GroupName()) {\n287: \t\t\t\tunknownExcluded.Delete(check.GroupName())\n288: \t\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(&individualCheckOutput, \"[+]%s excluded with %s: ok\\n\", check.Name(), check.GroupName())\n289: \t\t\t\tcontinue\n290: \t\t\t}\n291: \t\t\tif err := check.Check(r); err != nil {\n292: \t\t\t\tslis.ObserveHealthcheck(context.Background(), check.Name(), name, slis.Error)\n293: \t\t\t\t// don't include the error since this endpoint is public. Ready status is set after TSDB initialization completes and unset during graceful shutdown.\\n\\n### Comparison Summary\\n\\n| Aspect | Kubernetes | Grafana | Prometheus |\\n|--------|-----------|---------|------------|\\n| **Architecture** | Pluggable health checker framework | State-based readiness with database check | State-based with graceful shutdown tracking |\\n| **Liveness** | `/livez` with grace period | `/livez` (always 200) | `/-/healthy` (always 200) |\\n| **Readiness** | `/readyz` with rich checks | `/readyz` (state-based) | `/-/ready` (state-based) |\\n| **Dependencies Checked** | Informers, etcd, KMS, custom | Database connectivity | Internal initialization state |\\n| **Shutdown Support** | Explicit shutdown health check | (via HealthNotifier) | Dedicated Stopping state with header |\\n| **Response Format** | Text (\\\"ok\\\" or error list) | Text/JSON (database status, version) | Text (status message) |\\n| **Extensibility** | Add custom HealthChecker instances | Extend via HealthNotifier signals | Modify SetReady() calls in main |\\n\"\n   153→}\n   154→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware.
